\makeatletter
\pagestyle{plain}
\renewcommand{\@evenfoot}{\hfill\rotatebox{90}{\bf\qquad\qquad\thepage}}
\renewcommand{\@oddfoot}{\hfill\smash{\raise 27.8cm\hbox{%
  \rotatebox{90}{\bf\thepage}}}}

\newenvironment{CoupVec}%
  {\left[\begin{array}{>{\displaystyle}c}}%
  {\end{array}\right]}
\newenvironment{PlusB}%
  {\left\{\begin{array}{l}}%
  {\end{array}\right\}}
\newenvironment{PlusN}%
  {\begin{array}[t]{l}}%
  {\end{array}}

\def\Class#1#2{\par%
  \addcontentsline{toc}{subsection}{\texttt{[#1]} #2}%
  \fbox{\Large\texttt{[#1]}~~\textbf{#2}}\\[3ex]%
  \nopagebreak\bigskip\ignorespaces%
}

\def\Mfunction#1{\displaystyle #1}
\def\Muserfunction#1{\text{#1}}
\def\Mvariable#1{\text{#1}}
\def\InvisibleSpace{}

\def\Bar#1{\setbox0=\hbox{$#1$}\rlap{\raise\ht0\hbox{$-$}}\box0}
\def\nbox#1{\rlap{\lower 2ex\hbox{\scriptsize #1}}}
\def\i{\mathrm{i}}

\Class{FFS}{2 Charginos -- Higgs}
\nbox{251}$
\Mfunction{C}(\tilde \chi_{\Mvariable{c1}}^{-},\tilde \chi_{\Mvariable{c2}}^{+},h^{0}) = \Mfunction{ }
\begin{CoupVec}
\frac{\i\,e}{{\sqrt{2}}\,s_{W}}\,\left( s_{\alpha}\,U_{\Mvariable{c1},2}^{*}\,V_{\Mvariable{c2},1}^{*} - c_{\alpha}\,U_{\Mvariable{c1},1}^{*}\,V_{\Mvariable{c2},2}^{*} \right) \\
\\[-3ex]
\frac{\i\,e}{{\sqrt{2}}\,s_{W}}\,\left( s_{\alpha}\,U_{\Mvariable{c2},2}\,V_{\Mvariable{c1},1} - c_{\alpha}\,U_{\Mvariable{c2},1}\,V_{\Mvariable{c1},2} \right) 
\end{CoupVec}
$\\
\bigskip
\nbox{252}$
\Mfunction{C}(\tilde \chi_{\Mvariable{c1}}^{-},\tilde \chi_{\Mvariable{c2}}^{+},H^{0}) = \Mfunction{ }
\begin{CoupVec}
-\frac{\i\,e}{{\sqrt{2}}\,s_{W}}\,\left( c_{\alpha}\,U_{\Mvariable{c1},2}^{*}\,V_{\Mvariable{c2},1}^{*} + s_{\alpha}\,U_{\Mvariable{c1},1}^{*}\,V_{\Mvariable{c2},2}^{*} \right) \\
\\[-3ex]
-\frac{\i\,e}{{\sqrt{2}}\,s_{W}}\,\left( c_{\alpha}\,U_{\Mvariable{c2},2}\,V_{\Mvariable{c1},1} + s_{\alpha}\,U_{\Mvariable{c2},1}\,V_{\Mvariable{c1},2} \right) 
\end{CoupVec}
$\\
\bigskip

\\[-3ex]
\frac{e}{{\sqrt{2}}\,s_{W}}\,\left( s_{\beta}\,U_{\Mvariable{c2},2}\,V_{\Mvariable{c1},1} + c_{\beta}\,U_{\Mvariable{c2},1}\,V_{\Mvariable{c1},2} \right) 
\end{CoupVec}

\nbox{247}$
\Mfunction{C}(\tilde \chi_{\Mvariable{n2}}^{0},\tilde \chi_{\Mvariable{n1}}^{0},h^{0}) = \Mfunction{ }
\begin{CoupVec}
-\frac{\i\,e}{2\,c_{W}\,s_{W}}\,\left( s_{\alpha}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n1},3}^{*}\,\left( s_{W}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n2},1}^{*} - c_{W}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n2},2}^{*} \right)  + c_{\alpha}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n1},4}^{*}\,\left( s_{W}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n2},1}^{*} - c_{W}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n2},2}^{*} \right)  + \left( s_{W}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n1},1}^{*} - c_{W}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n1},2}^{*} \right) \,\left( s_{\alpha}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n2},3}^{*} + c_{\alpha}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n2},4}^{*} \right)  \right) \\
\\[-3ex]
-\frac{\i\,e}{2\,c_{W}\,s_{W}}\,\left( Z_{\Mvariable{n1},4}\,\left( c_{\alpha}\,s_{W}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n2},1} - c_{\alpha}\,c_{W}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n2},2} \right)  + Z_{\Mvariable{n1},3}\,\left( s_{\alpha}\,s_{W}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n2},1} - c_{W}\,s_{\alpha}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n2},2} \right)  + \left( s_{W}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n1},1} - c_{W}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n1},2} \right) \,\left( s_{\alpha}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n2},3} + c_{\alpha}\,Z_{\Mvariable{n2},4} \right)  \right) 
\end{CoupVec}

\end{CoupVec}

\Class{VVVV}{4 Gluons}
\nbox{401}$
\Mfunction{C}(g,g,g,g) = \Mfunction{ }
\begin{CoupVec}
-4\,\Mvariable{Alfas}\,\pi \,\i\,\left( f^{\Mvariable{g1},\Mvariable{g3},x}f^{x,\Mvariable{g2},\Mvariable{g4}} - f^{\Mvariable{g1},\Mvariable{g4},x}f^{x,\Mvariable{g3},\Mvariable{g2}} \right) \\
\\[-3ex]
-4\,\Mvariable{Alfas}\,\pi \,\i\,\left( f^{\Mvariable{g1},\Mvariable{g2},x}f^{x,\Mvariable{g3},\Mvariable{g4}} + f^{\Mvariable{g1},\Mvariable{g4},x}f^{x,\Mvariable{g3},\Mvariable{g2}} \right) \\
\\[-3ex]
4\,\Mvariable{Alfas}\,\pi \,\i\,\left( f^{\Mvariable{g1},\Mvariable{g2},x}f^{x,\Mvariable{g3},\Mvariable{g4}} + f^{\Mvariable{g1},\Mvariable{g3},x}f^{x,\Mvariable{g2},\Mvariable{g4}} \right) 
\end{CoupVec}
$\\
